ISPE Good Practice Guide: Single-Use Technology

Section 0: 1. Introduction & Key Concepts

導論與核心概念 | p7-p12

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Single-Use Technology | p7 - p12

本章學習目標

  • 理解 Single-Use Technology (SUT，單次使用技術) 的產業背景，以及它如何同時降低風險、縮短建廠時間並減少資本投入
  • 掌握本指引的目的與範圍，了解它涵蓋哪些應用場景（液態儲轉、細胞培養、填充封裝等），並清楚指引的使用前提
  • 熟悉本指引三大核心章節的結構：第2章組件選擇與設計、第3章導入與使用、第4章計畫管理
  • 精確掌握 SUT 關鍵詞彙的定義，區分 Extractables（萃出物）、Leachables（溶出物）、SUS、SUA 等易混淆概念
  • 理解毒理學相關閾值（AET、TTC、QT、SCT）的層級關係，為後續相容性評估建立基礎認識
  • 能夠辨別「Single-Use（單次使用）」與「Disposable（拋棄式）」兩個術語的實質差異，避免在 GMP 文件中混用
1.1 Background（背景）

原文內容 Original Text

The development of drug products from the laboratory to production processes entails risks, investment, and time. Any technology that can impact one or more of these factors is worth an investigation. Conventional stainless steel process equipment has reliably served the industry for many years. With the increasing need to reduce risks and quickly start up processing plants with minimum capital costs, Single-Use Technology (SUT) has been more widely used. This technology has impacted all three factors: risks, investment, and time.

The growth of SUT has been rapid and continues to expand in the industry. The primary components of SUT are polymeric film containers, flexible tubing, and an assortment of connectors and supporting components. The evolution of SUT has prompted the industry to redefine procedures to incorporate SUT into drug manufacturing processes. The application of this Guide starts after a decision to implement SUT is made; that is, all financial assessments have been completed and the results of those assessments support the use of SUT in a process. This Guide is aimed at helping the end-users and suppliers of SUT after this decision has been made.

While SUT provides flexibility, the implementation of SUT into a process requires a well-defined plan that minimizes surprises during the later stages of implementation. This can be a challenge when dealing with a revolutionary technology that is flexible, continues to evolve, and can be customized to the end-user's requirements. To take advantage of the flexibility of SUT, it is important to understand how the single-use products can work together with manufacturing operations. This Guide intends to provide a roadmap for the efficient implementation of SUT with minimum disruption to existing operations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：SUT 的三大驅動力

Single-Use Technology (SUT，單次使用技術) 之所以在生技製藥產業快速崛起，是因為它同時解決了傳統不鏽鋼設備的三大痛點：

  • Risk（風險）：免除清潔驗證 (cleaning validation) 的交叉污染風險，每批次使用全新設備
  • Investment（投資）：不需安裝固定管路、減少 CIP/SIP 基礎設施，資本支出大幅降低
  • Time（時間）：設施建置期縮短，特別適合臨床批次快速啟動或緊急藥品生產

本指引的適用起點：組織已完成財務評估，並決定採用 SUT——不討論「要不要用」，而是「怎麼用得好」。

比喻說明 Analogy

把 SUT 想像成「外送便當盒」對比傳統「瓷器餐盤」：瓷器餐盤耐用、可多次使用，但每次用完要清洗、消毒、檢查有無破損（對應 CIP/SIP + 清潔驗證）。外送便當盒用完即丟，省去清洗麻煩，但若亂選便當盒材質，食物可能吸收塑化劑——這正是 SUT 最大的合規挑戰：材料相容性與溶出物管控。

重點提示 Key Notes

原文強調 SUT 是「revolutionary technology that is flexible, continues to evolve」。這意味著法規指引永遠落後於技術發展，實務上需要仰賴供應商與使用者之間的緊密溝通，而非單純照抄法規條文。

CDMO 應用洞察

對於 CDMO（委託開發製造）而言，SUT 的靈活性尤其有價值：不同客戶的產品在同一廠房快速切換，SUT 的「用後即丟」特性天然解決了多產品廠的交叉污染疑慮，也大幅減少品種切換 (changeover) 的清潔驗證負擔——這是 CDMO 選擇 SUT 的核心商業理由。

1.2 Purpose and Objectives（目的與目標）

原文內容 Original Text

This Guide is centered around getting SUT implementation done right the first time, on schedule, and with minimal costs and few surprises. When surprises arise, this Guide aims to help address them effectively with the least amount of disruption.

This Guide aims to make it easier for single-use product suppliers and drug product manufacturers to select components and suppliers, design, and apply SUT. It intends to achieve this by aligning expectations and capabilities to minimize surprises.

Due to the inherent flexibility of SUT, the process of selecting, designing, and implementing SUT should be performed with sufficient focus while keeping the end state in clear perspective. During the design phase, there are many decisions to be made about the components to use. Focusing too closely on the decision at hand and putting the overall objective in second place can result in a decision that will need to be changed at a later date. The highly flexible nature of SUT allows this to be accomplished. However, it may result in a significant cost later in the project. If too many decisions are made in this way, the flexibility becomes its own hindrance. The objective of this Guide is to provide an efficient roadmap, based on the experience of the authors.

1.2.1 Scope

It is recognized that innovation and the fast evolution of SUT leads to a continuous expansion of available products. This Guide intends to capture the current technology, the components, and how they are designed into processes. The information presented is useful in the following applications:

  • Liquid or semisolid storage and transfer
  • Cell propagation and production of bulk biologics
  • Mixing of powders and liquids
  • Filtration and centrifugation
  • Heat transfer
  • Chromatography
  • Fill/finish

1.2.2 Benefits

The intended benefits of this Guide include:

  • Learning how to select single-use components and design functional systems
  • Learning when and how to perform effective extractables and leachables studies
  • Learning how to evaluate suppliers of SUT
  • Understanding the critical supplier and end-user (customer) interactions
  • Learning about the interrelated tasks for implementing SUT

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：「第一次就做對」的哲學

原文反覆強調 "done right the first time" 與 "minimize surprises"，這不只是口號，而是 SUT 專案失敗的主要模式：

  • 初期省略相容性測試 → 量產後發現溶出物超標 → 整批報廢
  • 組件設計時未考慮整體流路 → 後期需大幅修改組裝圖
  • 供應商未事先確認交貨週期 → 臨床批次延期

這份指引的核心價值：用別人踩過的坑，避免你自己重蹈覆轍。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUT 設計就像蓋房子：若設計師每次只看眼前的「這扇門要放哪裡」，而忘記整棟房子的動線，最後可能發現廚房門撞上冰箱。SUT 的高彈性（每個組件都可以更換）反而是個陷阱——越容易改，越容易在細節中迷失大局。

重點提示 Key Notes

範圍說明：本指引覆蓋從液態儲轉到 Fill/Finish 的完整 SUT 應用鏈。特別注意 Fill/finish（無菌分裝） 被明確列入範圍——這是無菌藥品製造 CDMO 最關鍵的應用場景，也是監管審查最嚴格的環節。

E&L 研究的重要性：「Learning when and how to perform effective extractables and leachables studies」被列為首要效益，可見 E&L 是 SUT 實施的核心技術門檻。

CDMO 應用洞察

對於無菌 Fill/Finish CDMO，SUT 的範圍直接涵蓋核心業務：袋裝灌裝、拋棄式過濾器、一次性管路系統。導入前必須建立清晰的供應商審核流程（第3章）與 E&L 評估標準（第2章），否則「靈活性」將演變為「不可控性」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠目前 SUT 應用覆蓋上表中的哪幾個場景？哪些場景尚未導入，原因是什麼？
  2. 在 SUT 導入專案中，你曾遇過哪些「事後才發現的驚喜 (surprises)」？如何在下個專案中提早識別？
1.3 Structure of the Guide（指引結構）

原文內容 Original Text

This Guide is intended to be used by those new to SUT while still benefiting those experienced with SUT. While any section of the Guide can be used at any time, those new to the technology would benefit by following a logical progression through the chapters. There are three core chapters. Chapter 2 guides the reader through component selection and equipment design. Chapter 3 takes the equipment into the plant and includes validation and training to yield a successful operation. Chapter 4 deals with program management topics that occur throughout the activities discussed in Chapters 2 and 3.

An overview of the Guide is as follows:

  • Introduction: This chapter provides the overall objectives of the Guide, background information on the technology, and the intended benefits of the Guide.
  • Selection and Design: Chapter 2 is intended to help the end-user select the components, assemblies, systems, and suppliers. The various sections in the chapter focus on identifying the major criteria for selecting the components for the single-use equipment and the suppliers that can support a successful SUT operation. The chapter details how assemblies are designed and aligned with the multiple-use parts of the system. Chapter 2 deals primarily with the first phase of any SUT implementation process. These activities require strong collaboration between the suppliers and the end-users. An emphasis is placed on how these collaborations are to be maintained and what information is expected to be shared between the two groups.
  • Implementation and Use: Chapter 3 covers topics which are to follow the completion of the activities of Chapter 2. Once the single-use assemblies, systems, and suppliers have been selected as described in Chapter 2, the focus is on using the single-use products in the end-user operation. Chapter 3 deals with the transfer of the technology into the plant, meeting regulatory requirements, training, validation, and setting up a strong supply chain. The end-users would take leadership in these activities with the supplier providing support.
  • Program Management: Chapter 4 mostly addresses planning information, including risk management, change management, and project schedules.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三章架構的邏輯

三大章節對應 SUT 導入的三個主要活動流：

  • 第2章 — 選擇與設計：供應商主導，使用者積極參與。重點是「選什麼」「如何設計」。
  • 第3章 — 導入與使用：使用者主導，供應商提供支援。重點是「如何讓它在工廠正常運作」——包含驗證、培訓、供應鏈。
  • 第4章 — 計畫管理：貫穿整個專案的橫向管理活動。風險管理、變更管理、時程控制。

這個架構反映了一個重要的責任分工原則：選購時供應商是專家，導入後使用者必須成為主人。

比喻說明 Analogy

這三章就像新廠開工的三個階段：第2章是「採購與設計圖」，第3章是「施工與驗收」，第4章是「專案經理全程盯場」。少了任何一章，都可能讓 SUT 專案功虧一簣。

重點提示 Key Notes

原文強調「strong collaboration between the suppliers and the end-users」——SUT 不是買了就能用的產品，而是需要雙方持續溝通的合作關係。這意味著採購合約中必須明確規範「資訊共享義務」，包括材料變更通知、批次測試數據、E&L 研究結果等。

CDMO 應用洞察

CDMO 在 SUT 供應鏈中扮演雙重角色：對客戶而言是「製造服務提供者」，對 SUT 供應商而言是「高要求的技術終端使用者」。建議建立 SUT 供應商資格管理 (Supplier Qualification) 程序，將第2、3章的要求轉化為內部 SOP，並在客戶技術協議中明確 SUT 相關的品質責任分工。

1.4 Key Concepts/Terms — 毒理與相容性術語（第一組）

原文內容 Original Text

Analytical Evaluation Threshold (AET)

Analytical Evaluation Threshold (AET): An upper limit, at or above which, identification and quantification of an unknown extractables and leachables should be performed and reported for potential toxicological assessment. This is not applicable to special case compounds such as Polyaromatic Hydrocarbon (PAH, also known as polynuclear aromatic hydrocarbons), Mercaptobenzothiazole (MBT) and N-nitrosamine, which should be evaluated individually.

Compatibility

Compatibility: A measure of the extent to which a Primary Packaging Component (PPC), Process Contact Material (PCM), and/or proximal material will interact with a dosage form. Such interaction should not be sufficient to cause unacceptable changes in the quality of either the dosage form or the packaging component. Such interactions may include (ab)adsorption of the active drug substance, reduction in the concentration of an excipient, leachable-induced degradation, precipitation, changes in drug product pH, discoloration of the dosage form or packaging component, etc.

Container Closure System (CCS)

Container Closure System (CCS): The sum of packaging components that together contain, protect, and deliver the dosage form. This includes primary packaging components and secondary packaging components if the latter are intended to provide additional protection relative to product stability to the drug product (e.g., foil pouch).

Extractables

Extractables: Chemical compounds that are removed from a material by exertion of an artificial, exaggerated force (e.g., solvent, temperature, or time). This is a material specific characteristic and is independent of the drug product with which the material is used.

Leachables

Leachables: Chemical species that migrate from or through a contact surface into a drug product or process stream during storage or normal use conditions. These are specific to the combination of material and drug product with which the material comes in contact.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：E&L 的根本差異

Extractables（萃出物） 與 Leachables（溶出物） 是 SUT 安全評估的核心雙概念，必須嚴格區分：

  • Extractables：在「極端條件」（高濃度溶劑、高溫、長時間）下從材料中強制萃取出的化合物。是材料本身的特性，與實際產品無關。由供應商提供測試數據。
  • Leachables：在「實際使用條件」（正常儲存、正常接觸）下遷移進入藥品的化合物。是材料 + 藥品組合的特性，必須針對具體產品測試。

簡單記憶：Extractables 是「最壞情況」，Leachables 是「真實情況」。Leachables 通常是 Extractables 的子集。

核心概念：AET 的作用

Analytical Evaluation Threshold (AET，分析評估閾值) 是分析化學與毒理學的橋樑：AET 之上的未知化合物，必須進行鑑別、定量，並報告進行潛在毒理評估；AET 之下的化合物，可以「報告但不鑑別」。

例外情況（需個別評估）：PAH（多環芳烴）、MBT（巰基苯并噻唑）、N-亞硝胺——這三類是已知的高毒性/致癌物，不適用「低濃度可忽略」的邏輯。

比喻說明 Analogy

把 CCS（容器封閉系統）想像成「藥品的家」：主包材（PPC）是直接接觸藥品的「臥室牆壁」，次包材是「外牆」——外牆若能額外隔熱（保護產品穩定性），也算 CCS 的一部分（如鋁箔袋）。相容性 (Compatibility) 評估就是確保「房子材料不會汙染居住者」。

重點提示 Key Notes

相容性 的評估範圍非常廣：不只是「材料會不會溶出毒素」，還包括活性成分被吸附 (adsorption/absorption)、輔料濃度下降、pH 變化、外觀變色等。這些互動即使不涉及毒性，也可能導致產品不符規格——同樣是 CAPA 的來源。

CDMO 應用洞察

在無菌 Fill/Finish CDMO，每個新產品引入新的 SUT 組件前，必須有書面的相容性評估計畫。建議在技術轉移 (Technology Transfer) 審查中明確要求客戶提供或委託執行 E&L 研究，並在批量生產前完成 Leachables 確認。這是降低批次報廢風險的關鍵管控點。

1.4 Key Concepts/Terms — 組件、系統與閾值術語（第二組）

原文內容 Original Text

Primary Packaging Component (PPC)

Primary Packaging Component (PPC): A component of the container closure system that potentially comes into direct contact with the drug product formulation (e.g., canisters, pumps, actuators, gaskets, syringe plungers, stoppers, etc.).

Process Contact Material (PCM)

Process Contact Material (PCM): Component which is in direct contact with the process or product fluid, such as tubing, hose, filter, bag, connector, etc. Also known as process stream contact material.

Proximal Materials

Proximal Materials: All packaging materials other than the PPC, such as ink, adhesive, label, carton, protective packaging materials, etc.

Qualification Threshold (QT)

Qualification Threshold (QT): A level below which a given leachable is not considered for safety qualification (toxicological assessment) unless the leachable presents Structure-Activity Relationship (SAR) concerns.

Safety Concern Threshold (SCT)

Safety Concern Threshold (SCT): A level below which a leachable would have a dose so low as to present negligible safety concerns from carcinogenic and non-carcinogenic toxic effects.

Single-Use Assembly (SUA)

Single-Use Assembly: A combination of single-use components/assemblies designed to be in one continuous, and often closed, wetted flow path. The typical assembly is manufactured and sterilized. It primarily contains mechanical components (e.g., bioprocess container, tubing, fittings, etc.) with sensor element(s) or allowance for a sensor element to be mounted by the end-user. The end-user places the assembly on a support structure prior to filling it with fluid. The support structure may also include electromechanical elements (e.g., mixer/motor, bag lift, scale, bag carrier, etc.) that interface with the assembly and are integral for its proper use.

Single-Use System (SUS)

Single-Use System (SUS): A combination of single-use components designed to be in one continuous, and often closed, wetted flow path. The typical SUS integrates one or several single-use assemblies with multiple-use electrical/control elements operated by some level of automation. The end-user places the single-use assembly on a support structure prior to filling it with fluid.

Single-Use Technology (SUT)

Single-Use Technology (SUT): Technology based on applications that utilize single-use components individually or in assemblies and systems that are designed based on these components. Figure 1.1 provides an overall perspective on the relationship between components, assemblies, and systems.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：SUT 層級架構（Component → Assembly → System）

SUT 有清晰的三層結構，必須明確區分：

  • Component（組件）：最基本單元——管件、接頭、濾器、袋子
  • Single-Use Assembly (SUA，單次使用組合件)：多個組件組合成一條完整的濕潤流路 (wetted flow path)，出廠前已滅菌。是 SUT 的核心交付物。
  • Single-Use System (SUS，單次使用系統)：SUA + 多次使用的電控/自動化元件的整合體。SUS 是「軟硬兼施」的完整操作單元。
  • SUT：最廣義的術語，涵蓋以上所有層級的技術概念。

關鍵區別：SUA 是「用完即棄的部分」；SUS 中的電控部分（馬達、感測器）是可重複使用的。

核心概念：毒理閾值的層級關係

溶出物安全評估有三個閾值，由嚴格到寬鬆：

  • SCT（安全關注閾值）：最嚴格的底線。低於此值，無論致癌或非致癌毒性均可忽略不計。
  • QT（資格閾值）：低於此值，免除毒理評估——除非有 SAR（構效關係）疑慮。
  • AET（分析評估閾值）：分析化學層面的觸發點，達到或超過此值的未知物才需要鑑別量化。

通常 SCT ≤ QT ≤ AET——數值越低，要求越嚴格。

比喻說明 Analogy

PPC 與 PCM 的區別：PPC 是「裝藥品的容器」（針劑注射器活塞、瓶塞），強調的是包裝完整性與最終產品接觸；PCM 是「製程中接觸藥液的管道」（軟管、濾膜、生物反應袋），強調的是製程流路中的接觸。兩者都需要 E&L 評估，但監管要求的框架略有不同（ICH Q3D、USP <661> vs BPOG/ASTM E55 系列）。

重點提示 Key Notes

Proximal Materials（鄰近材料） 常被忽視：標籤油墨、黏合劑、外盒紙板也可能透過間接途徑遷移影響藥品品質，尤其對於高滲透性包材（如某些聚合物袋）。ICH Q3D 及 USP <1664> 均有對應的鄰近材料評估要求。

SAR（構效關係）：即使某化合物濃度低於 QT，若其化學結構顯示潛在致突變性，仍需個別評估。這是 PAH、MBT、N-亞硝胺被排除在 AET 通用規則外的原因。

CDMO 應用洞察

在 SUT 供應商評估中，應要求供應商提供完整的 AET/QT/SCT 計算依據，以及 SUA 的 E&L 研究報告（通常依照 BPOG 方法論）。CDMO 的品質協議中應明確規定供應商在材料變更時的提前通知義務，因為任何 PCM 材料變更都可能觸發重新 E&L 評估，影響客戶的藥品上市時程。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠目前如何管理 SUT 供應商的材料變更通知？是否有 SOP 明確要求供應商在變更前提前告知？
  2. 在評估新 SUT 供應商時，你會要求哪些 E&L 相關文件？如何判斷供應商提供的 Extractables 數據品質？
1.4 Key Concepts/Terms — 其他重要術語（第三組）

原文內容 Original Text

Single-Use versus Disposable

While these terms seem to be used interchangeably, there are significant differences between them. Single-use products are a subset of disposable products. Single-use products are used one time and then discarded. They are typically used for the duration of a process run. At the end of a process run, any drug product is displaced from the single-use product and then the single-use product is discarded. Disposable products are often used only once and discarded. However, disposable products may also be used more than once. If the disposable product is to be used more than once, it is cleaned and sanitized between uses. Performance should be monitored as it normally decreases with each sequential use. Exposure to cleaning chemicals and high temperatures tends to degrade the disposable products resulting in a limited useful life.

Support Equipment/Systems

Support Equipment/Systems: Support systems that are used in conjunction with single-use equipment. These include temperature control systems for heating/cooling media and restricted access barrier systems.

Threshold of Toxicological Concern (TTC)

Threshold of Toxicological Concern (TTC): The daily intake of a genotoxic impurity that is considered to be associated with an acceptable risk (excess cancer risk of < 1 in 100,000 over a lifetime) for most pharmaceuticals.

Toxicological Assessment

Toxicological Assessment: An evaluation of the estimated Total Daily Intake (TDI), which is considered similar to the Average Daily Intake (ADI) of a chemical species, in order to determine if the level of exposure will present a safety concern to the patient. These evaluations include considerations of available literature data for the specific compound or class of compounds, SAR, and any qualification data (if available).

Tubing Set

Tubing Set: An assembly composed of single-use components that is used to connect between unit operations.

Upstream/Downstream Processing

Upstream/Downstream Processing: Upstream processing includes the unit operations up to the harvest clarification and recovery from the bioreactor. Downstream processing includes the unit operations that follow such as the filtration and chromatography steps to purify and concentrate the product.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：Single-Use vs Disposable 的關鍵區別

這是業界最常見的混用術語，必須在 GMP 文件中嚴格區分：

  • Single-Use（單次使用）：一個製程批次 (process run) 使用一次，批次結束即棄。不進行清潔，不考慮二次使用性能。這是 SUT 的本質定義。
  • Disposable（拋棄式）：廣義概念，包含單次使用，但也包括可以多次使用後再棄置的產品。多次使用的 Disposable 需要清潔、消毒，且性能隨使用次數遞減。

實務啟示：若 GMP 文件寫「disposable tubing set」，監管審查員可能詢問「是否驗證過多次使用的性能」——改寫為「single-use tubing set」可避免此歧義。

核心概念：TTC 的毒理學定義

Threshold of Toxicological Concern (TTC，毒理關注閾值)：針對基因毒性雜質，設定每日攝取量低於此閾值時，終生癌症超額風險 < 1/100,000 是可接受的。TTC 是 ICH M7 基因毒性雜質指引的核心概念，與 SUT 的 E&L 安全評估直接相關——當溶出物被懷疑具基因毒性時，需與 TTC 比較。

比喻說明 Analogy

Upstream/Downstream 的簡單記憶法：把生物製程想像成「上游：農場（種植細胞、培養生長）→ 下游：食品工廠（純化、濃縮、配製）」。上游在生物反應器（Bioreactor）收穫之前；下游從收穫後的過濾、層析、配製，一直到無菌分裝。SUT 在兩個階段均有廣泛應用，但各有側重的組件類型。

重點提示 Key Notes

Support Equipment/Systems 雖非 SUT 本身，但直接影響 SUT 的操作可靠性。例如，受限進入屏障系統 (Restricted Access Barrier System, RABS) 與一次性手套口袋的接口設計，是無菌 Fill/Finish 的關鍵整合點。溫控系統（加熱/冷卻）若失效，可能影響 SUT 組件的機械完整性，進而引發系統洩漏。

CDMO 應用洞察

無菌 Fill/Finish CDMO 的 SUT 最關鍵應用點恰好橫跨 Downstream 的末端——無菌過濾、灌裝管路、容器密封系統均屬 SUT 範疇。TTC 的概念提醒我們：對於高注射劑量（如靜脈輸注）的生物製劑，Leachables 的可接受限度比口服製劑嚴格得多，計算 AET 時的假設劑量必須基於最壞情況的臨床給藥途徑。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠 SOP 中，是否明確使用「single-use」還是「disposable」？如果兩者混用，在下次 SOP 修訂時應如何標準化術語？
  2. 在計算溶出物的 AET 時，如何確定「最壞情況 (worst-case) 每日攝入量」？給藥途徑（靜脈 vs 皮下）對計算結果有多大影響？

本章重點摘要 Chapter Summary

  • SUT 的三大價值主張：降低風險（免清潔驗證）、減少投資（輕型基礎設施）、縮短時程（快速啟動）。本指引的前提：組織已決定採用 SUT，目的是「如何做對」而非「要不要做」。
  • 指引架構：第2章（選擇與設計）→ 第3章（導入與使用）→ 第4章（計畫管理）。三章形成完整的 SUT 實施生命週期框架，第4章貫穿始終。
  • 術語精確性：Single-Use ≠ Disposable；SUA（組合件）≠ SUS（系統）；Extractables（實驗室強制萃取）≠ Leachables（實際使用遷移）。在 GMP 文件和供應商協議中必須嚴格使用正確術語。
  • 毒理閾值層級：SCT（最嚴）→ QT（次嚴）→ AET（分析觸發）。TTC 針對基因毒性化合物適用，PAH/MBT/N-亞硝胺需個別評估，不適用通用閾值邏輯。
  • CDMO 核心關注點：E&L 評估是 SUT 導入的技術門檻，供應商變更管理是供應鏈風險的主要來源，SUT 的靈活性若缺乏系統化設計思維，反而成為專案延誤的根源。
  • 供應商與使用者協作：選購階段供應商主導，導入後使用者必須成為主人。資訊共享、材料變更通知、技術支援邊界——這些都需要在品質協議中事先書面化。
1a

Section 1a: 2.1–2.2: Components & Extractables

元件與可萃取物 | p13-p28

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Single-Use Technology | p13 - p28

本章學習目標

  • 區分單次使用元件（Single-Use Components）、組件系統（SUS）三個層次的定義，掌握浸濕元件與非浸濕元件的分類邏輯
  • 熟悉主要單次使用元件的功能與特性——包括生物工藝袋、管路、連接器、過濾器、感測器、閥件等——以及它們在無菌充填流程中的應用場景
  • 理解可萃取物（Extractables）與可瀝出物（Leachables）的本質差異，掌握 E&L 研究在藥品安全評估中的核心地位
  • 掌握可萃取物研究的設計空間概念，包括 QbD 原則、臨界應用分層、PCM/PPC/CCS 的層級架構
  • 了解可萃取物測試的方法論——模擬溶劑選擇、萃取參數設定、分析技術（GC-MS、LC-MS、ICP-MS）及 AET 接受標準判斷
  • 建立 CDMO 視角的 E&L 風險管理思維：從供應商數據審查、責任矩陣分工到毒理評估結論的完整工作流程
2.1 Single-Use Components, Assemblies, and Systems（單次使用元件、組件系統總覽）

原文內容 Original Text

This section lists the single-use products that are commonly used in pharmaceutical manufacturing facilities. Aligned with Figure 1.1, single-use products can be categorized as follows:

  • Single-use components represent the single-use parts that may be used individually or as a subset of an SUS
  • Single-use assemblies consist of multiple single-use components connected in various configurations to make a unit operation in the manufacturing process
  • SUSs integrate single-use components/assemblies with multiple-use parts
Note: This section is intended to cover components, assemblies, and systems most commonly used in SUT and is not intended to be a comprehensive listing.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三層架構——元件 → 組件 → 系統

ISPE SUT 用清晰的三層分類架構來描述單次使用技術的範疇：

  • 元件 (Component)：最小單位，例如一截管路、一個連接器
  • 組件 (Assembly)：多個元件組合成一個製程操作單元，例如「過濾組件」= 過濾器 + 管路 + 連接器
  • 系統 (SUS)：組件 + 多次使用設備（如不鏽鋼框架、泵浦驅動器）整合而成的完整設備

這個三層架構對 E&L 研究非常重要——萃取研究通常從元件層次開始，再擴展到系統層次的浸出研究。

比喻說明 Analogy

把這三層想成蓋房子：元件 = 磚頭、鋼筋（個別材料）；組件 = 一堵牆、一個房間（功能單元）；系統 = 整棟建築（含水電設備的完整設施）。做材料安全測試時，先測磚頭的化學析出，再測整棟建築的室內空氣品質。

CDMO 應用場景

在 CDMO 的日常作業中，三個層次的管理責任不同：

  • 元件：由供應商提供 CoA（成分証明）與 E&L 資料包
  • 組件：通常由 CDMO 或供應商依 URS 客製化組裝，需進行完整性測試
  • 系統：CDMO 負責設備確效（IQ/OQ/PQ）及操作 SOP
2.1.1 Single-Use Components（單次使用元件）

原文內容 Original Text

Components can be classified into two categories, based on whether the surface(s) will be exposed to a fluid (liquid or gas) when in service:

  • Wetted components contact the product or process fluid
  • Non-wetted components do not contact the product or process fluid but may be in contact with wetted components

Wetted components may be further classified based on their potential contact time with product or process fluid, as shown in Figure 2.1.

Bioprocess Bags（生物工藝袋）

Bioprocess bags (also referred to as single-use bioprocess containers) are flexible containers that are made of polymeric material and intended to be used once and discarded. The main applications are storage, sampling, mixing, freezing, and transport of liquids. Other applications include cell culture, fermentation, and powder storage/transfer.

These containers have inlet/outlet ports with fittings and associated tubing. The smaller bioprocess bags (typically 30 mL to 50 L) are typically two-dimensional (2-D) and expand like a pillow or sack when filled. As the sizes get larger (typically 100 L to 3,000 L), the bioprocess bags are three-dimensional (3-D) and typically match the shape of the bag container they will be placed into during use (e.g., stainless steel support structures/frames or totes).

Bottles（瓶）

Bottles are rigid plastic vessels with volumes that typically range from 1 L to 20 L. Applications for bottles include sampling, storage, and freezing. They may be reusable (multiple-use) for non-critical applications.

Impellers/Mixers（攪拌器）

Impellers/mixers are used to agitate fluid in a container. Common types include:

  • Impeller with magnetic or magnetic-like drive
  • Impeller with levitating drive
  • Mechanical mixing (e.g., paddle or agitator shaft)

Tubing（管路）

Tubing is manufactured from flexible polymer material and used for fluid transfer with or without pumping. Tubing is available in various diameters, lengths, wall thickness, and shore hardness. Materials of construction vary and include fluoropolymers, thermoplastics, and silicones. Thermoplastic tubing can be heat sealed (for aseptic disconnection) and welded (for tube/tube aseptic connection). Certain types of tubing are specifically designed to be used with peristaltic pumps or to withstand high pressures.

Port Fittings（接口配件）

Port fittings are heat sealed to the chamber portion of a bioprocess bag and used to connect tubing, allowing for fluid to enter or exit the bags. Port fittings can also be found on bottles, and these would normally be accompanied by a seal.

Connectors（連接器）

Tubing connectors contain hose barb fittings, and may be used to connect tubing of different materials of construction and/or diameter sizes:

  • Two pieces of tubing with straight connector
  • Three pieces of tubing with T or Y shape connector
  • Four pieces of tubing with + shape connector

Connectors vary depending on the type of application:

  • When ease of use is important but aseptic connections are not required: Luer-Lok® connectors, quick connects, and sanitary clamp fittings (Tri-Clamp®). These connectors may be handled within a laminar flow cabinet (ISO 5/Grade A conditions) if aseptic connections are required.
  • When aseptic connections are required, the connectors should prevent any interaction between the fluid and the outside environment:
    • Equal complementary elements (genderless connectors): two elements that are exactly alike and interchangeable
    • Matched complementary elements (gendered connectors): two elements that are matched and can only be connected together

Steam-in-place connectors may be used between single-use components and stainless steel systems.

Disconnectors（斷開器）

Disconnectors are used to make aseptic disconnections:

  • Fluid path aseptic disconnectors: need to be pre-assembled on the single-use assembly, usually through hose barb fittings
  • Non-fluid path disconnectors: can be pre-installed or standalone, based on an external part that is pressed and cut to allow aseptic disconnection

Filter Capsules（過濾器）

Filter capsules of numerous types are used in single-use assemblies. Filters may be classified by:

  • Filtration mode: dead-end filtration versus tangential flow filtration
  • Type of filtration: Sterilizing grade / Pre-filtration / Depth filtration
  • Materials of construction
  • Configuration: Parallel plate / Pleated membranes / Non-woven / Hollow fiber
  • Filter media features: Polymer type (e.g., cellulose acetate, polyamide, polyether sulfone, PVDF, PTFE, PP, PE, glass fiber), filter pore size, filter surface area, Hydrophobic/Hydrophilic
  • Connection style: Hose barb / Sanitary

Valves（閥）

Valves are used to direct the flow of fluid either as wetted components or as controlled constrictions acting on tubing. There are also simple pinch valves that have a decreasing channel that squeezes the tubing to control the flow.

Sensors（感測器）

Sensors of several types have been specifically developed to be single-use and can be integrated into single-use assemblies. Currently available single-use sensor types include:

  • Conductivity / Dissolved Oxygen (DO) / Flow / pH / Pressure / Temperature

For applications where single-use sensors are not available, multiple-use sensors may be used via aseptic connections or sealed barrier. Common multiple-use sensor types include: Dissolved gases / Level / Mixing speed / Turbidity / UV absorbance / Weight (load cells).

Other Components（其他元件）

Pump liners are polymeric components within the pump that make up the fluid path and create pressure; replaced after each use. Centrifuge liners are polymeric liners designed for use in centrifuge systems. Gaskets and O-rings are used in connections between sanitary fittings, within valves, and between two solid components. Materials include EPDM, PTFE, Viton®, and silicone. Filling needles are used in final filling operations, primarily made of stainless steel. Chromatography components include pre-packed columns (usually not single-use) and membrane chromatography equipment (usually single-use). Clamps and fasteners are non-wetted components used to secure tubing connections.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：浸濕 vs 非浸濕元件

這個分類對 E&L 研究至關重要。浸濕元件（Wetted）直接接觸產品或製程液體，是潛在化學污染的來源，必須進行完整的可萃取物研究。非浸濕元件（Non-Wetted）如夾具、扣件，雖不直接接觸液體，但若透過浸濕元件間接傳遞，也需要評估。

進一步，浸濕元件依接觸時間分層——靜態長時間接觸（如儲存袋）與動態短時間接觸（如生物反應器袋）的 E&L 風險截然不同，需採用不同的萃取條件。

關鍵元件：生物工藝袋 (Bioprocess Bag)

生物工藝袋是 SUT 中體積最大、E&L 最受關注的元件。幾個關鍵參數：

  • 材質：多層聚合膜（通常含 LDPE、EVA 等），各層功能不同（阻隔層、強度層、接觸層）
  • 2-D vs 3-D：30 mL–50 L 為 2-D 枕型；100 L–3,000 L 為 3-D 需不鏽鋼支撐框架
  • 伽馬輻照：預滅菌處理，但輻照會改變聚合物化學特性，可能增加可萃取物——這是 E&L 研究的關鍵輸入

關鍵元件：管路 (Tubing)

管路是 SUT 中面積最廣的液體接觸元件，也是蠕動泵磨損的直接對象：

  • 矽膠管 (Silicone)：柔性好，生物相容性佳，蠕動泵首選，但有氧化矽浸出風險
  • 氟聚合物管 (Fluoropolymer)：化學惰性強，適合高溶劑耐受需求，但較硬
  • 熱塑性管 (Thermoplastic)：可熱封/熱焊接，實現無菌連接與斷開

關鍵元件：無菌連接器 (Aseptic Connectors)

無菌連接器是 SUT 的一大競爭性創新領域，關鍵區別：

  • 無性別連接器 (Genderless)：任一件可與另一件配對，庫存管理簡單
  • 有性別連接器 (Gendered)：公/母配對，設計上能防止錯誤連接
  • 蒸汽原位連接器 (SIP)：用於 SUT 與傳統不鏽鋼系統的橋接點

重點提示：過濾器的關鍵分類

在無菌製程中，最關鍵的是除菌過濾（Sterilizing Grade），孔徑 ≤0.22 μm，需通過 ASTM F838 泡點測試與細菌截留測試驗證。

切向流過濾（TFF）用於超濾/濃縮製程，流路設計複雜，通常作為預設計組件提供，不適合臨時拼裝。

比喻說明：感測器的單次 vs 多次選擇

想像一次性快篩試劑（單次感測器）vs 實驗室分析儀（多次感測器）：快篩方便但精確度有限；分析儀精確但需要清潔校準。在 SUT 中，pH、溶氧等單次感測器的精度已大幅提升，但部分高精度應用（如濁度、UV 吸收）仍仰賴多次感測器透過無菌隔膜插入。

CDMO 應用場景：元件選型決策樹

在 CDMO 接新客戶 tech transfer 時，元件選型需考量：

  • 客戶原廠使用的品牌是否與我方供應商兼容？（連接器介面標準化）
  • 產品接觸元件的 E&L 數據包是否符合 ICH Q3D 元素雜質、AET 要求？
  • 伽馬輻照劑量是否符合廠內驗收規格？（通常 25–45 kGy）
  • 蠕動泵管路是否通過 pump tubing validation（磨損微粒測試）？

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在你的充填工廠，哪些元件屬於「浸濕 + 長接觸時間」的高風險類別？供應商的 E&L 數據包是否涵蓋伽馬輻照後的條件？
  2. 你工廠現有的管路材質組合是什麼？有無混用矽膠管與熱塑性管的場景？連接點如何保持無菌？
2.1.2 Single-Use Assemblies（單次使用組件）

原文內容 Original Text

Single-use assemblies can range from relatively simple units (such as buffer bag assemblies) to complex units (such as bioreactor assemblies). Examples of single-use assemblies include:

  • Buffer storage assemblies
  • Mixer assemblies
  • Sample manifold assemblies
  • Transfer manifold assemblies
  • Bioreactor assemblies
  • Filtration assemblies
  • Chromatography assemblies
  • Centrifuge assemblies
  • Fill/finish manifold assemblies

Single-use assemblies are available as standardized products or may be customized for specific process needs. Considerations should be made to design single-use assemblies that can be used in multiple steps within a manufacturing facility, benefiting the overall operation in terms of flexibility and minimization of inventory.

2.1.2.1 Bioprocess Bag Assemblies

Bioprocess bags are often bulky and impact space requirements for storage areas. Selecting standardized (versus customized) bags and connections can help to reduce inventory levels, since one assembly design can potentially be used in multiple steps in the process.

  • 2-D Bioprocess Bags: Standard specifications include tubing dimensions for the integral tubing and standardized connectors for sampling. Use of standard designs is recommended to minimize cost and provide flexibility between assemblies.
  • 3-D Bioprocess Bags: Most tubing entry points for the larger 3-D bioprocess bags are from the top. Care should be taken when adding auxiliary components to these entry points as they may require special handling to protect the bag surface.

During selection of the bioprocess container, attention should be taken to ensure that the minimum mixing volume is met and that ample ports are available for additions and sampling.

2.1.2.2 Manifolds

Manifolds can range from being straightforward to complex in design. They are commonly the second bulkiest portion of the assembly, after the bioprocess bag. Aspects of manifold design and selection include:

  • Sizing of tubing diameters and minimizing lengths and bends are important for proper fluid handling.
  • The pressure rating of the tubing should be matched for the application; reinforced tubing is available for applications above the pressure rating of standard tubing.
  • Welds and aseptic connections should be used as needed to maintain sterility and flexibility.
  • For processes that allow ports to be combined, manifolds can allow the use of standard bioprocess containers without modifications to the number of connections.

2.1.2.3 Filter Assemblies

Typical assemblies consist of normal flow filters (dead-end filters) that are relatively small (less than 10 inch). Depending on whether the application is an open or closed operation, vent filters may be required on bioprocess containers. Vent filters on bioreactors are typically full size capsule filters provided in a redundant pair with heated jackets. Tangential flow filters are commonly incorporated into pre-designed assemblies to allow for special flow paths required for their operation.

2.1.2.4 Filling Assemblies

Final filling assemblies are specially designed filter assemblies that account for factors such as:

  • Venting the filters in a sterile manner
  • Filter flush collection
  • Low particulate requirements
  • Peristaltic pump tubing, if required
  • Surge bags, if required
  • Single-use needles, if required

2.1.2.5 Mixer Assemblies

Mixer assemblies can also range from simple to complex in design, due to the need for different mixing requirements, probes, avoidance of dead legs, and sampling requirements. Mixer types include bottom mount agitator, top mount agitator, and pump around. There are also different options for how the single-use impeller is coupled to the motor; special attention should be made for high viscosity, high solids, or low particulate applications.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：組件設計的標準化 vs 客製化取捨

選擇標準化組件的優勢：庫存品項少、可跨製程步驟共用、供應鏈穩定、E&L 數據已驗證。選擇客製化組件的場景：製程有特殊接口需求、客戶指定供應商、清洗/滅菌方式特殊。

ISPE 指引的建議方向：能標準化就標準化——這也是 CDMO 降低 COGs（Cost of Goods）的關鍵策略之一。

關鍵概念：管路岐管 (Manifold) 設計要點

Manifold 是多條流路匯集或分流的核心組件，設計不良會導致：

  • 死角 (Dead Leg)：流體停滯區域，微生物生長的溫床——管路長度不得超過管徑 6 倍原則
  • 壓力損失：彎頭過多或管徑驟縮導致壓降不符預期
  • 完整性風險：連接點過多，每個焊接點或連接器都是潛在洩漏點

重點提示：充填組件的特殊性

充填組件（Filling Assembly）是整個無菌製程中風險最高的組件，原因：

  • 距離最終產品最近，無任何後續稀釋或過濾步驟可降低風險
  • 微粒要求最嚴格——任何橡膠磨耗、矽膠粒子都可能成為注射用藥品的異物
  • 蠕動泵管路需通過 pump wear validation，確認微粒脫落在可接受範圍

這呼應了 2.2.4.3 節的「臨界應用分層」原則：充填步驟屬最高風險等級。

比喻說明：混合組件的攪拌器選擇

想像三種廚房攪拌方式：頂部安裝攪拌器（如家用桌上攪拌機）適合中等黏度、需要開口加料；底部安裝攪拌器（如咖啡機研磨）適合密閉系統、較均勻的流體；泵循環（Pump Around）（如魚缸過濾泵）適合大體積、輕柔混合怕剪力的生物製劑（如 mAb 原液）。選錯攪拌方式，蛋白質聚集就發生了。

CDMO 應用場景：Filling Assembly 的風險管理

在一次性充填系統的驗證中，CDMO 的實務工作項目包括：

  • 管路蠕動泵磨耗測試（>10 小時模擬運轉後取樣分析微粒）
  • 充填針材質相容性確認（不鏽鋼 316L vs 聚合物充填針）
  • Surge bag 對充填速率穩定性的影響評估
  • 過濾器排氣程序無菌驗證（防止排氣期間外界汙染進入）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠的充填線組件是標準化還是客製化？更換供應商時需要重新進行哪些驗證項目？
  2. Manifold 設計中如何避免死角？你現有的 SOP 對死角管理有什麼規定？
2.1.3 Single-Use Systems（單次使用系統）

原文內容 Original Text

SUSs, as shown in Figure 1.1, are comprehensive units. SUSs are composed of single-use components/assemblies and multiple-use parts. In general, the multiple-use parts are used to:

  • Support and provide mobility to the single-use assemblies
  • Control the motion of fluids within and between single-use assemblies
  • Monitor operating conditions
  • Provide process controls for the unit operation or to the entire manufacturing process

The multiple-use parts in an SUS are often complex equipment and considerations should be made to how they interface with single-use components/assemblies. For example, wear or deformation of multiple-use parts can have disastrous impact on the integrity of the single-use components.

Multiple-use parts represent conventional equipment, which are not covered in this Guide. To help the end-user select the appropriate equipment for SUSs, this Guide highlights concepts and criteria in Section 2.3 (Process Equipment Design).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：SUS 中的多次使用設備風險

SUS 最容易被忽略的風險點：多次使用設備（Multi-Use Parts）對單次使用元件完整性的影響。

  • 蠕動泵的泵頭磨耗 → 管路受力變形 → 管壁變薄 → 爆破風險
  • 不鏽鋼支撐框架的銳角或毛邊 → 袋體刮破 → 完整性失效
  • 閥門驅動器的扭矩過大 → 管路受壓不均 → 洩漏

這意味著 SUS 的確效不只是測試一次性組件，更要確認多次使用設備在正常磨耗範圍內不影響組件完整性。

CDMO 應用場景：SUS 確效的範疇界定

在制定 SUS 的 IQ/OQ/PQ 計畫時，需明確界定：

  • 哪些部件是「單次使用組件」（每批更換，供應商負責 E&L 數據）
  • 哪些部件是「多次使用設備」（需要設備確效，CDMO 自行維護）
  • 兩者界面（Interface）的完整性測試頻率與方法

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠使用的生物反應器系統（如 Sartorius Biostat® 或 Thermo Fisher HyPerforma™）中，哪些是多次使用設備？這些設備的磨耗如何影響一次性袋體的完整性？
  2. 當多次使用設備送去保養維修時，回廠後需要進行哪些確效再確認步驟？
2.2 Extractables（可萃取物）——概論

原文內容 Original Text

Single-use products are made from polymeric materials; one of the key elements to qualifying and implementing such a material is to understand and control the impacts of using it within a defined process. Extractable and leachable (E&L) profiles are a main part of this required impact assessment.

Note: Although "extractables and leachables" is commonly used as one term, these concepts reflect two distinctly different ways of determining the chemical species that may migrate from the component:
  • Extractables are removed from the component by exaggerated force, involving high temperatures, high and low pH, and aggressive solvents; this information can be useful for assessing the risk of the component in any application.
  • Leachables, on the other hand, are a result of the interaction of the production within the equipment; therefore, related studies use actual product and process conditions to determine which chemical components will migrate from the component. When actual product is not possible, a mimic of the product might be used.

A science and risk-based approach to an extractables study is recommended due to its complexity and the need for trace level analysis. Risk factors include, but are not limited to: surface area to volume ratio, extracting potential of the process stream or formulation, and duration of exposure. For example, a storage bag may be static in process contact but long in duration, while a bioreactor bag may be dynamic in process contact but short in the duration of contact.

Because this Guide deals with SUT applied in the processing of products which are intermediates, the focus of this section is on extractables as it applies to process contact materials (PCM), and not to finished dosage forms or containers.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：Extractables vs Leachables——根本差異

這是 SUT 最重要的概念區分，考試和法規審查中極常被混淆：

  • 可萃取物（Extractables, E）：在「誇張條件」下（高溫、極端 pH、有機溶劑）強制萃取出的化學物質。目的是建立材料的「化學指紋庫（Chemical Fingerprint）」，代表最大可能的化學風險。類似「刑事審訊」——逼出所有可能的化學物。
  • 可瀝出物（Leachables, L）：在實際製程/產品條件下自然遷移出的化學物質，代表真實的患者暴露風險。類似「日常接觸」——真實環境下的實際釋出量。

邏輯關係：Extractables ⊇ Leachables（可萃取物是可瀝出物的超集）。先做 E 研究，再用 E 的結果預測 L 的風險，決定是否需要進一步的 L 研究。

風險評估的關鍵參數

E&L 風險 ∝ 表面積/體積比 (SA/V) × 萃取潛力 × 接觸時間

高風險場景：小體積 + 大面積接觸（如充填管路）
低風險場景：大體積 + 短接觸時間（如轉移袋，接觸 ≤1 hr）

AET（Analytical Evaluation Threshold）計算：
AET = SCT × (重量/天用量) × (1/提取效率)
SCT = Safety Concern Threshold（ICH Q3D 或毒理 TTC 值）

比喻說明：E vs L 就像食品包裝測試

想像一個塑膠水瓶：可萃取物研究就像把水瓶泡在熱水 + 酒精 + 酸液中強制萃取——測試最壞情況下會析出什麼物質；可瀝出物研究就像把水瓶裝水在常溫放 6 個月，再測水的成分——測試實際使用條件下你喝到了什麼。前者是安全底線研究，後者是現實風險確認。

重點提示：CDMO 作為中間製程的特殊性

原文特別指出，本指引的 E&L 重點是製程接觸材料（PCM），而非最終劑型容器。這對 CDMO 很重要：

  • CDMO 處理的是「藥物中間體（Drug Substance）」，不是直接接觸患者的最終產品
  • 但某些製程步驟（如原液充填到 DS 儲存袋）的 E&L 數據可能被 MAH（上市許可持有人）要求納入法規申請
  • 需明確在客戶合約中界定 E&L 數據的提供責任

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠的哪個製程步驟具有最高的 SA/V 比？現有的 E&L 評估是否涵蓋了這個步驟的最壞條件？
  2. 當客戶提問「你們的一次性儲存袋有 E&L 數據嗎？」，你的標準回應流程是什麼？由誰提供哪些文件？
2.2.1 Roles and Responsibilities（角色與責任分工）

原文內容 Original Text

Extractables studies represent one of the most challenging aspects of pharmaceutical development. There is a large degree of complexity given by the number of factors that influence an extractables evaluation. The involvement of teams with adequate skills and subject matter expertise from both end-users and suppliers help in tackling each factor efficiently.

Table 2.1 provides a template of the typical deliverables responsibilities matrix for an extractables study. Allocation of these responsibilities varies depending on company policy and procedures.

R=Responsible, A=Accountable, C=Consulted, I=Informed

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：RACI 矩陣在 E&L 研究中的應用

RACI 矩陣（Responsible / Accountable / Consulted / Informed）是跨組織協作的標準工具。在 E&L 研究中，端用者（End-User = CDMO/製藥公司）與供應商之間的責任劃分是最容易造成糾紛的環節。

從表 2.1 可以看出幾個關鍵原則：

  • URS 定義：端用者主導（A/R），供應商只是 Informed——這意味著你必須先知道自己需要什麼，再要求供應商提供
  • 萃取程序執行：供應商主導（A/R），端用者全部是 Informed——供應商的實驗室能力是關鍵
  • 毒理評估：端用者 Quality/Regulatory 是 R，SME 是 A——毒理結論的責任在用戶端

重點提示：SME（Subject Matter Expert）的角色

E&L 研究需要的跨領域專業：

  • 分析化學：GC-MS、LC-MS、ICP-MS 方法開發與驗證
  • 毒理學：TTC（Threshold of Toxicological Concern）評估、ICH Q3D 元素雜質風險評分
  • 聚合物科學：了解特定聚合物的已知降解產物（例如矽膠的環狀矽氧烷 D4、D5）
  • 法規事務：ICH Q3D、USP <661>、EP 3.1、FDA/EMA E&L 指引的要求對照

對於不具備完整 SME 能力的 CDMO，通常需要委外給專業的毒理 CRO 進行評估。

CDMO 應用場景：供應商審核中的 E&L 問卷

在供應商資格審核（Supplier Qualification）時，應要求提供：

  • E&L 研究報告摘要（是否涵蓋目標應用的萃取條件）
  • 使用的分析方法與偵測極限（LOD/LOQ）
  • 是否已通過 AET 評估，並提供毒理評估結論
  • 批次間變異性數據（至少 3 批）
  • 伽馬輻照後的 E&L 數據是否包含在報告中

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠現在的 SUT 供應商審核流程中，有無要求 E&L 數據包？如果沒有，從哪個步驟開始補充最有效率？
  2. 毒理評估（Toxicological Assessment）在你的組織由誰負責？是內部 QA/RA 還是委外 CRO？各有什麼限制？
2.2.2 Pre-requirements（前提要求）

原文內容 Original Text

Components which are planned for an extractables study should first meet the following regulatory and pharmacopeial expectations:

  • Requirements for polymeric materials:
    • Plastic polymers used in manufacturing single-use components should not contain natural rubber, latex, or special case compounds (PAH, N-nitrosamines, and MBT)
    • USP <381> Elastomeric Closure for Injection
    • USP <661> Plastic Packaging Systems and Their Materials of Construction
    • European Pharmacopoeia (EP) General Chapter 3.1 Materials Used for the Manufacture of Containers
  • Requirements for major compendia:
    • USP <87> Biological Reactivity, In Vitro — in vitro testing is a minimum requirement
    • USP <88> Biological Reactivity, In Vivo — in vivo testing is preferred
    • EP 3.2.9, JP Section 7.03, and corresponding ISO 10993-1 tests for in vitro and in vivo testing
  • Animal derived Stearates: EU Commission Decision 97/534/EC

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：E&L 研究的門檻前提

進行正式 E&L 研究之前，材料必須先通過這些「基礎資格審查」——就像應聘工作需先有基本學歷門檻才能進入面試環節。

最關鍵的禁用成分：

  • 天然橡膠/乳膠：過敏原，注射用藥品絕對禁用
  • 多環芳烴 (PAH)：致癌物，來源通常是碳黑或礦物油潤滑劑
  • N-亞硝胺 (N-Nitrosamines)：ICH M7 基因毒性雜質，極低 TTC（1.5 μg/天）
  • MBT（苯並噻唑）：橡膠硫化促進劑，潛在致癌物

CDMO 應用場景：供應商 CoA 審查要點

收到新批次一次性組件時，在 CoA 審查中確認：

  • 材料聲明（Material Declaration）：有無聲明不含乳膠/PAH/N-亞硝胺/MBT
  • USP <87>/<88> 測試結果（合格/Passes）
  • EP 3.1 或等效聲明
  • 動物源性原料聲明（如含硬脂酸鹽，需符合 97/534/EC）
2.2.3 Risk Assessment in Extractables Study（可萃取物研究的風險評估）

原文內容 Original Text

In defining requirements for the design of extractables studies, the risk management tools described in ICH Q9 should be employed. For example, application of quality risk management would consider:

  • If an automated component manufacturing process is used
  • If the process has been satisfactorily audited
  • If a smaller sample may be needed, as opposed to a manually intensive manufacturing and/or inspection process for the component which may dictate a larger sample because of higher probability of variability

SUS extractables testing approach and methodology should be determined based on scientific knowledge and regulatory expectations. Decision trees and other risk assessment tools should be implemented at an early stage of the extractables study definition.

The purpose of these studies is to obtain extractables profiles of SUS components considered as PCM in direct contact with the process or product fluid. The risk assessment should consider both patient safety (with regard to the impact of extractables compounds on product quality and safety) and the overall process performance. Extractables studies should integrate regulatory expectations as inputs of the risk assessment. Patient safety should be considered by suppliers in the development of single-use components, and by end-users in the implementation of these components in the drug manufacturing process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：ICH Q9 風險管理在 E&L 研究的應用

ICH Q9 的核心工具（FMEA、HACCP、風險矩陣）在 E&L 研究中的具體應用：

  • 自動化製造 vs 手工製造：自動化製程批次間變異小，可能允許減少批次數；手工製程變異大，需要更多批次樣本覆蓋
  • 化學指紋庫（Chemical Fingerprint）：E&L 研究的最終目標——建立每個一次性元件的「身份 DNA」，包含所有潛在遷移物的定性定量數據

重點提示：雙重責任視角

原文強調供應商和端用者各有責任：

  • 供應商責任：在元件開發階段就考慮患者安全，選擇低遷移性聚合物，提供完整的 E&L 數據包
  • 端用者責任（CDMO）：在將元件導入製程時進行風險評估，確認供應商的 E&L 數據適用於自身的製程條件（溫度、pH、接觸時間可能與供應商的標準測試條件不同）

這是最常見的風險盲區——供應商的標準萃取條件未必涵蓋 CDMO 客戶的特定製程條件。

CDMO 應用場景：E&L 風險評估矩陣建立

建議依以下維度建立 E&L 風險矩陣：

  • 接觸時間：<1 hr（低）/ 1–24 hr（中）/ >24 hr（高）
  • 接觸面積：SA/V 比 <1 cm⁻¹（低）/ 1–10 cm⁻¹（中）/ >10 cm⁻¹（高）
  • 製程位置：上游（低）/ 下游（中）/ 充填前（高）
  • 溫度：室溫（低）/ 37°C 培養（中）/ >50°C（高）

矩陣評分決定需要的 E&L 研究深度（供應商數據即可 / 需要補充研究 / 需要完整自主研究）。

2.2.4 Design Space（設計空間）

原文內容 Original Text

2.2.4.1 Basis for Comparative Evaluation

The starting point for an extractables study should be a review of the supplier's data. Ideally, these studies should be performed on materials at the component level, under standardized conditions of temperature, time, surface area, etc. (so the data are comparable) which are representative of the intended use, including steam sterilization or gamma irradiation. Using this data, the end-user can then calculate the maximum amount of extractables based on the surface area and other conditions in the process.

2.2.4.2 Extractables Study Design Space

The extractables study should be developed based on Quality by Design (QbD) principles described in ICH Q8 to gather all attributes and parameters that enter into the determination of a design space. Scientific variables should be identified to set up Design of Experiment (DOE) for the extraction procedure.

2.2.4.3 Critical Applications

Different requirements of the extractables study could be applied depending on the criticality of application, context, and utilization of SUS components, as illustrated in Figure 2.2 (Criticality Scale of Industrial Application).

Figure 2.3 provides a high-level overview of the development stages in a typical biological manufacturing process, in relation to increased risk associated with materials safety requirements; that is, the closer the single-use component is to the fill/finish step, the less opportunity that risk mitigation (such as dilution or filtration) can take place.

2.2.4.4 Primary Packaging Component, Process Contact Material, and Container Closure Systems

Extractables studies are usually performed on individual PPCs (Primary Packaging Components) and PCMs (Process Contact Materials), as a precursor step to leachables studies which are performed on entire systems considered as CCSs (Container Closure Systems). E&L studies should demonstrate the safety and chemical compatibility of the CCS, PCM, and proximal materials used in the processing and intermediate storage of a drug substance.

The duration of exposure to these materials varies greatly depending upon the specific process. Compatible packaging and contact materials should not cause changes to the efficacy, potency, and safety of the drug product.

2.2.4.5 Decision Tree for Approval of Materials Based on Extractables Study

Figure 2.5 illustrates typical key aspects that should be considered in the approval of materials based on an extractables study. The decision tree guides whether extractables data is acceptable, or whether further toxicological assessment or targeted studies are required.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：QbD + DOE 在 E&L 研究中的應用

ICH Q8 的 QbD 精神應用到 E&L 研究：

  • 關鍵品質屬性（CQA）：哪些可萃取化合物對患者安全有影響？（毒理篩選確定）
  • 關鍵製程參數（CPP）：溫度、pH、接觸時間、SA/V 比這些參數如何影響萃取量？
  • 設計空間（Design Space）：在哪些參數範圍內，可萃取物濃度始終低於 AET？
  • DOE 設計：系統性地改變萃取條件（例如 2×2 因子設計：低溫/高溫 × 低 pH/高 pH），找到最壞條件組合

關鍵概念：CCS / PPC / PCM 的層級關係

這三個縮寫在法規文件中頻繁出現，必須清楚區分：

  • CCS（容器密封系統）：最廣義——整個容器+密封系統，是 ICH Q1B、ICH Q3B 研究的對象
  • PPC（初級包裝元件）：直接接觸最終藥品的包裝材料（如西林瓶、膠塞、鋁蓋）
  • PCM（製程接觸材料）：製程中接觸中間體的材料（SUT 的主要研究對象）

在生物製劑 CDMO 中：
PCM = 一次性袋體、管路（DS 製造階段）
PPC = 西林瓶、膠塞（DP 充填後）
CCS = 西林瓶 + 膠塞 + 鋁蓋整體系統

臨界應用分層邏輯

製程位置對 E&L 風險的影響：

上游（細胞培養/發酵）
  ↓ 多道純化步驟可去除遷移物
  ↓ 離子交換層析、病毒過濾、超濾
  ↓
下游（純化後原液）
  ↓ 僅剩一道除菌過濾
  ↓
充填/封裝（Fill/Finish）← 最高風險
  ↓ 無後續去除機制
  ↓ 直接進入最終產品

原則：距充填越近 → E&L 要求越嚴格

重點提示：從供應商數據到端用者計算

供應商的 E&L 數據通常以「每單位面積萃取量（μg/cm²）」表示。端用者（CDMO）需要將其換算成實際製程暴露量：

實際暴露量（μg/L）= 供應商數據（μg/cm²）× 實際 SA（cm²）÷ 批次體積（L）

再與 AET 比較，決定是否需要額外的特定目標研究（Targeted Study）。

CDMO 應用場景：決策樹的實務執行

當 E&L 評估結論出現以下情況時的標準處理路徑：

  • 計算暴露量 < AET：記錄評估結論，無需額外測試，定期審查
  • 計算暴露量 > AET 但有毒理數據支持：進行完整毒理評估，記錄風險接受理由
  • 計算暴露量 > AET 且無充分毒理數據：考慮更換供應商、更換元件材質、或補充特定目標 E&L 研究
  • 存在已知基因毒性化合物：即使低於一般 AET，需符合 ICH M7 規定（TTC 1.5 μg/天）
2.2.5 Key Recommendations for Extractables Study（可萃取物研究的關鍵建議）

原文內容 Original Text

Extractables should be readily identified, quantified, and evaluated for their impact on drug quality (and consequently patient safety) arising from the interaction between process fluids (simulated by model solvents) and polymeric PCM. In the extractables study, the single-use component is considered as PCM. The objective is to obtain a chemical fingerprint of the tested single-use components. The information from the extractables study should be used to support the selection of raw materials in the single-use component manufacturing process.

The overall approach to conducting an extractables study is:

  • Benchmarking of previous extractables testing protocols and results for comparable single-use components
  • Determination of acceptance criteria based on user requirements, the intended design and use of the single-use component, and scientific literature
  • Performing the extraction procedure on the single-use component to be tested
  • Comparison of actual results to acceptance criteria and performing toxicological assessment with conclusion

2.2.5.1 Requirements for Processing and Storage of PPC/PCM

The PPC and PCM should be processed in the same manner in which they will be processed for use in manufacturing. This includes steps such as washing, lubrication/coating, packaging, and sterilization. They should be held at their specified storage conditions, or as otherwise justified.

2.2.5.2 Requirements for Including Proximal Packaging Components

Packaging components and materials which do not directly contact the drug product should be evaluated on a case-by-case basis for their potential to leach chemicals into the dosage form. Polymeric containers with a glass transition temperature below room temperature have a high potential for migration of chemical entities through them. Packaging components (such as label stock, carton, adhesives, inks, varnishes, and lacquers) should be included in the overall extractables evaluation due to the potential for migration through the polymeric material.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：化學指紋庫（Chemical Fingerprint）

E&L 研究的最終交付物是一份「化學指紋庫」，包含：

  • 已鑑定化合物的清單（定性——GC-MS、LC-MS 鑑定）
  • 各化合物的濃度（定量——與 AET 比較）
  • 毒理評估結論（是否需要進一步關注）

這份指紋庫具有材料特異性——換了供應商、換了批次樹脂、改了製造製程，都需要重新評估指紋庫是否仍然適用。

核心概念：滅菌條件對 E&L 的影響

2.2.5.1 特別強調元件在萃取測試前應已完成與實際使用相同的處理程序，其中滅菌最關鍵：

  • 伽馬輻照（Gamma Irradiation）：輻射能量引發聚合物鏈斷裂和自由基反應，可能產生新的分解產物（如矽膠中的低分子量環狀矽氧烷 D4/D5）
  • 高壓蒸汽滅菌（Autoclave）：高溫高濕可能加速水解，從聚合物中析出添加劑
  • 環氧乙烷（EtO）：EtO 殘留及其反應產物（乙二醇、乙烯氯醇）需要納入 E&L 評估

重點提示：近端包裝材料（Proximal Packaging）的風險

這個常被忽略的風險點：外包裝（紙箱、標籤、黏著劑、油墨）中的化學物質可能穿透玻璃轉化溫度低於室溫的聚合物容器，最終遷移至內容物。常見的高風險化合物：

  • 印刷油墨中的光起始劑（Photoinitiators）：如 ITX（isopropylthioxanthone）——著名的 Isociate 污染事件
  • 黏著劑溶劑：甲苯、乙酸乙酯的殘留
  • 紙板中的礦物油：MOH（Mineral Oil Hydrocarbons）污染

比喻說明：滅菌改變 E&L 就像烹飪改變食物

未烹飪的生雞肉（未滅菌元件）和烤雞（伽馬輻照後元件）的化學成分截然不同。你不能用生雞肉的「食品安全分析」來代表烤雞的安全性。同樣地，供應商的 E&L 數據必須明確標示是輻照前還是輻照後的數據，兩者不可互換。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你現有的 SUT 供應商提供的 E&L 數據是在伽馬輻照前還是後測試的？輻照劑量是否與你廠接收規格一致？
  2. 你的一次性儲存袋外層包裝有無使用含有機溶劑的油墨？玻璃化轉變溫度是多少？有無進行過近端包裝的遷移評估？
2.2.6 Extractables Testing（可萃取物測試）

原文內容 Original Text

2.2.6.1 Selection of PPC/PCM Lots

Where practical, extractables studies of PPC, PCM, and proximal materials should be designed to capture lot-to-lot variability (preferably different resin lots, if possible). Multiple lots of PPC/PCM are recommended, when possible, for extractables evaluation. Non-consecutive lots, if available, should be used in the studies.

Consideration should be made for the large supplier lots that may be received at the end-user facility on different dates or purchase orders. These may be identified as different lots, but in fact are not reflective of supplier process variability. To determine whether or not multiple lots are needed, an assessment of the point of variability in the supply chain (e.g., manufacturing, batch processing, washing, sterilizing, etc.) should be conducted.

The mass to volume ratio and sample size of the PPC/PCM are important inputs to extractables characterization. Sample preparation should be consistent in geometry for the different PPC/PCM lots. Consideration can also be made to use a small-scale model for execution of the extractables study to support qualification of the large-scale model. However, the mass to volume ratio should be maintained as close as possible to the ratio of the original intended size.

2.2.6.2 Extraction Conditions and Procedures

Extraction conditions are critical in determining the chemical profile and levels of individual extractables. Prior to the execution of the extraction procedure, critical factors should be determined. An extractables assessment should provide quantitative and qualitative assessment of the safety threshold for individual extractables. The assessment should be based on different key factors, including:

  • Fluid path characterization
  • Nature of single-use components
  • Manufacturing process conditions

These factors are illustrated in Figure 2.6 (Ishikawa principle/Fishbone Diagram), which enables study design and extraction strategies.

The manufacturing process should be evaluated with regard to process conditions, proximity to the final product, and pretreatment procedures (e.g., autoclaving or gamma irradiation).

These critical factors help to determine extraction conditions, which are based on parameters including:

  • Chemical nature of the extracting media (model solvent)
  • Duration of the extraction process and the temperature
  • Stoichiometry of the extraction process: surface area to volume ratio; mass of individual extractable compounds extracted per surface ratio
  • Physical characteristics of the extraction method

2.2.6.3 Extraction Parameters

The extraction conditions (including temperature, pH, and time) should be appropriately selected, well described, and justified. Extraction media may include a drug product vehicle and organic solvents of varying polarities, extreme pH, and extreme ionic strength.

Considerations for extraction parameters include:

  • Selection of appropriately aggressive solvents, rather than simulating the action of the fluid path
  • Performing extractable analysis with multiple substitute solutions — each solution should approximate the effect of one or more of the physical and chemical properties of the fluid path
  • Selection of model solvents based on variability of polarities — the power of model solvent extraction and their variabilities ensure the largest range of extractable compounds are encompassed
  • Volatility of the solvent as a key concern regarding extraction factor and the compatibility of the solvent with the analytical method
  • Determining the volume of extraction media using the surface area of the component in contact with the process fluid path (only the inner surface area in contact with the extraction media is considered)

2.2.6.4 Testing Methodology

The levels of the identified extractable compounds should be analyzed and compared to standard guidelines such as the ICH Q3D, EP General Chapter 3.1, and USP <661>. Common analytical techniques used in extractables testing include:

  • GC-MS (Gas Chromatography–Mass Spectrometry): for volatile and semi-volatile organic compounds
  • LC-MS (Liquid Chromatography–Mass Spectrometry): for non-volatile and polar compounds
  • ICP-MS (Inductively Coupled Plasma–Mass Spectrometry): for elemental impurities (metals)

In addition, refer to a proposed standardized extractables protocol (Ding et al., 2014).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：批次選擇的科學依據

「非連續批次（Non-Consecutive Lots）」的設計邏輯：想要捕捉的是供應商的製程變異（樹脂批次、製造時間、滅菌參數），而非同一大批次的分割。

常見陷阱：採購了 3 批一次性袋，但其實是同一批樹脂在同一週內生產的——這 3 批並不代表真正的批次間變異。正確做法：要求供應商提供不同樹脂批號的產品。

關鍵概念：模擬溶劑（Model Solvents）的選擇邏輯

模擬溶劑的選擇依據極性梯度，覆蓋不同類型的化學遷移物：

ISPE 的建議：使用表面積（而非質量）來決定萃取溶劑體積，確保 SA/V 比的一致性。

AET（分析評估閾值）計算

AET 定義：低於此濃度的萃取物無需進一步毒理關注

計算公式（簡化）：
AET = SCT ÷ (日劑量體積 × 萃取效率)

其中：
SCT = Safety Concern Threshold
  - 一般有機物 TTC = 1.5 μg/天（Kroes et al.）
  - ICH Q3D 元素雜質：依元素毒性分類（PDE 值）
  - 基因毒性化合物（ICH M7）= 1.5 μg/天

示例：
日劑量體積 = 100 mL
SCT = 150 μg/天（一般有機物上調係數後）
萃取效率 = 50%
AET = 150 ÷ (0.1 L × 0.5) = 3,000 μg/L = 3 ppm

比喻說明：Ishikawa（魚骨圖）在 E&L 研究設計

用魚骨圖分析影響萃取結果的因素，就像調查事故根因：主幹是「萃取物濃度」，六根骨頭分別是「溫度」、「pH」、「接觸時間」、「SA/V 比」、「溶劑種類」、「元件特性」。系統性地評估每根骨頭，才能設計出覆蓋所有最壞條件的 DOE 實驗方案。

CDMO 應用場景：接受供應商 E&L 數據的確認清單

當供應商提交 E&L 報告時，CDMO QA 應確認：

  • 測試批次是否使用了非連續批號（≥3 批）
  • 萃取條件是否涵蓋你的製程最壞條件（最高溫度、最長接觸時間、最大 SA/V）
  • 報告中的 AET 計算是否基於你的產品每日劑量（Different products = different AETs！）
  • GC-MS、LC-MS、ICP-MS 三項分析是否都已執行？LOQ 是否低於 AET 的 1/5？
  • 所有鑑定化合物是否都有毒理結論（通過/需關注/需進一步測試）？
  • 如有超出 AET 的化合物，是否提供了完整的毒理評估（HHE）？

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你工廠目前使用的一次性儲存袋供應商，是否提供了包含 GC-MS + LC-MS + ICP-MS 三種分析的完整 E&L 報告？報告中的萃取條件是否覆蓋了你的最高儲存溫度？
  2. 如果要為新引進的 mAb 原液儲存袋計算 AET，你需要哪些輸入數據？你的毒理評估流程是什麼？由誰負責最終結論？

本章重點總結 Chapter Summary

  • 三層架構：單次使用技術分為元件（Component）→ 組件（Assembly）→ 系統（SUS）三個層次。浸濕元件是 E&L 研究的主要對象，非浸濕元件也需進行間接影響評估。
  • 元件多樣性：生物工藝袋（2-D/3-D）、管路（矽膠/氟聚合物/熱塑性）、無菌連接器（有性別/無性別）、過濾器（除菌/深層/切向流）、感測器（單次/多次）等元件各有其設計特點與限制，選型需考量製程相容性和 E&L 數據完整性。
  • E vs L 根本差異：可萃取物（Extractables）用「誇張條件」強制萃取，代表最大化學風險上限；可瀝出物（Leachables）用實際製程條件，代表真實患者暴露量。前者先行，後者依需要補充。
  • 風險分層原則：製程位置越靠近充填步驟，E&L 要求越嚴格——因為稀釋和過濾等風險緩解機制越少。充填組件屬最高風險等級，需最完整的 E&L 評估。
  • 分析三劍客：GC-MS（揮發性有機物）、LC-MS（非揮發性極性有機物）、ICP-MS（元素雜質）三項分析技術聯合使用，才能覆蓋完整的化學指紋庫。AET 是判斷是否需要進一步毒理關注的關鍵閾值。
  • CDMO 的雙重責任：作為端用者，CDMO 必須建立明確的供應商 E&L 數據審查流程（RACI），確認供應商的萃取條件與自身製程最壞條件的相關性，並對毒理評估結論承擔最終責任。
1b

Section 1b: 2.3–2.4: Equipment Design & Quality

設備設計與品質要求 | p29-p50

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Single-Use Technology | p29 - p50

本章學習目標

  • 掌握 SUT 感測器、閥門、泵浦、生物反應器等製程設備的設計考量，理解各類設備的選型邏輯與限制
  • 理解單次使用系統的環境需求分類——開放式、封閉式、功能性封閉製程的差異，以及對潔淨室等級要求的影響
  • 掌握 SUT 品質要求的三個層次：單次使用組件、組合件、系統，各層次的品質要求重點與差異
  • 理解濕面 (wetted) / 非濕面 (non-wetted) 組件的分類概念，以及對應的品質要求差異（生物負荷、內毒素、微粒、完整性測試等）
  • 熟悉供應商評估矩陣的應用——從組件供應商到組合件供應商到系統供應商的多層次管理架構
  • 掌握品質管理系統方法：QbD (ICH Q8)、QRM (ICH Q9)、CoC / CoQ 文件要求，以及終端使用者的進料檢驗實務
2.3 Process Equipment Design （製程設備設計）— 概述

原文內容 Original Text

This section focuses on the design aspects of process equipment design and the operational characteristics of single-use components for implementation of SUT. The topics that are addressed in this section include: sensors, single-use valves, pumps, single-use assemblies, bioreactors, environmental requirements, and considerations for control systems, utility and process support, maintenance and calibration, safety, and cleaning.

Choosing the appropriate components can be one of the most challenging aspects of implementing SUT, especially for transitions from traditional clean-and-reuse systems. Creating detailed user requirements at the beginning of the project is essential in determining which single-use components are suitable for the application. In selecting equipment, primary consideration should be given to suitability with the process. Considerations should also be given to equipment flexibility, customization options, future scale-up requirements, and supplier support.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：製程設備設計的挑戰

從傳統不鏽鋼設備轉向 SUT，最難的地方不是技術，而是選擇適合的組件。傳統系統幾十年來已有標準規格，但 SUT 市場仍在快速演進，沒有「一套通吃」的標準。

這一節的邏輯是：先有 User Requirements（使用者需求），再根據需求評估哪些 SU 組件「適配」製程。適配性 (Process Suitability) 是第一優先，而非品牌或成本。

比喻說明 Analogy

就像裝修新廚房——你不是直接去建材行買最貴的設備，而是先想清楚「我每天要煮幾個人的飯、用什麼烹飪方式、廚房有多大空間」。SUT 選型也一樣：先寫 URS（使用者需求規格書），再去找能滿足需求的供應商。

CDMO 應用情境

在 CDMO 環境下，同一設施可能服務不同客戶的製程。選擇 SUT 組件時要特別考慮彈性——能否適用於不同製程流體？能否支援不同批量規模？這直接影響設備投資的回收效率。

2.3.1 Sensors （感測器）

原文內容 Original Text

The determination of the level of accuracy needed (as compared to what the traditional system can measure) is important, as sensors may vary in accuracy and cost. For all single-use sensors, it is highly advised to test the accuracy and precision of the device in-house before implementation in the manufacturing facility.

Considerations for the selection of single-use sensors include:

  • Fundamental technology behind the sensor (e.g., a rotary flow meter measuring rotations by reflection of infrared light from rotor blades will not be reliable when used with colored solutions such as cell culture media)
  • Materials of construction (sensors exposed to process solutions and solvents should be assessed for chemical compatibility)
  • Compatibility with the desired sterilization method (e.g., chemical, radiation, thermal) to ensure that calibration is not affected
  • Calibration strategy (availability of pre-calibrated probes, if required)
  • Robustness of the measurement and drift level under actual conditions of use
  • Standardized connections (selection of components with specialized connections may result in being locked in with one supplier)
  • Allowance for the end-user to perform pre-use steps without breaking sterility

2.3.1.1 Level Sensors

Options for level measurements in SUSs include:

  • For hanging bags (with understanding of solution density): load cell strain gauge
  • For mixers and larger tanks: guided-wave radar, floor scale, and load cells
  • For bubble traps: gas/liquid detector

2.3.1.2 Flow Sensors

Options for flow measurements vary greatly in fixed cost, variable cost, and accuracy:

  • Rotary meters: typically less accurate (± 5%) and more affordable
  • Coriolis meters: more accurate (± 1%) and more expensive
  • Ultrasonic flow meters: easily moved but tend to be more expensive
  • Magnetic flow meters: good accuracy for mid-range expense but not usable with deionized liquids

2.3.1.3 pH Sensors

Options for pH measurements include:

  • Traditional pH sensors: Cleaned while connected to an aseptic connector half, then autoclaved. Accurate across the range used in biological operations.
  • Single-use pH sensors: For physiological range (pH 5.5–8.5), can be inserted into the flow path and gamma irradiated. Provides similar accuracy to traditional probes in this range.
  • Sensor spots: Chemical optical spots placed inside a clear bioprocess container before sterilization, read by a fiber optical cable. Limited pH range; certain cell culture media components can affect accuracy. The end-user should verify accuracy on their specific media, feeds, and buffers before implementation.

2.3.1.4 Dissolved Oxygen

The most straightforward way to bridge DO sensing from stainless steel to SUSs is to use traditional DO sensors (cleaned, then autoclaved). Single-use sensors using plastic sheath and optical sensing technology are available, with narrower range and higher detectability limit but similar accuracy in typical cell culture ranges.

2.3.1.5 Pressure

Several types of single-use pressure sensors are available. Main differences are accuracy, connection type (in-line vs. T), inner diameter, maximum pressure rating, and cost. Multiple-use gauges added onto single-use instrument Ts in a tubing set are also common. Calibration concerns may drive the need for a pre-use calibration depending on the criticality of the measurement.

2.3.1.6 Temperature / Conductivity

Most available sensors have accuracy of approximately 3%. The major differences between suppliers are operating conductivity ranges and available hose barb connection sizes. An alternative is a single-use conductivity probe pre-connected to a bioprocess bag, pre-calibrated, irradiated, providing 2% accuracy (100 mS/cm) via an integrated four-electrode system and temperature sensor.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：感測器選型的黃金原則

單次使用感測器不是把傳統感測器直接換成拋棄式這麼簡單——感測技術的根本原理決定了它在特定應用中是否可靠。

最容易忽略的陷阱：供應商鎖定 (Supplier Lock-in)。選擇使用專屬接頭的感測器，就等於把未來的採購選擇綁定在單一供應商。ISPE 明確建議優先選擇標準化接頭設計。

比喻說明 Analogy

紅外線旋轉流量計用有色培養基就會失準——就像用可見光測量深色玻璃後面的物體，顏色本身就會干擾讀值。這個例子提醒我們：感測器的物理原理決定了應用限制，不能只看規格表，要理解背後的量測機制。

流量計精度與成本比較框架

精度高低：Coriolis (±1%) > Ultrasonic > Magnetic > Rotary (±5%)
成本高低：Coriolis > Ultrasonic > Magnetic > Rotary
可移動性：Ultrasonic 最佳（夾管式，不需切斷管路）
限制注意：Magnetic 無法用於去離子水（無導電性）

重點提示：pH 感測器的實務陷阱

Sensor Spots（光學感測貼片）操作方便，但特定細胞培養基成分會影響讀值準確性。ISPE 特別提醒：正式導入前，終端使用者必須用自己的培養基、饋料液和緩衝液進行驗證，不能光靠供應商規格書。

在 GMP 生產環境，感測器的校正策略必須在驗證計畫中記載清楚——包括使用前校正、使用後確認，以及可接受的漂移範圍。

CDMO 應用情境：生物製程感測

在無菌充填的 CDMO 製程中，pH 和 DO 是上游生物反應器的關鍵參數。選擇 Single-use pH probe（可 gamma 照射）搭配 Single-use DO probe，可在不破壞無菌屏障的前提下完成 pre-use 安裝——對縮短批次切換時間（Changeover Time）非常關鍵。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的設施目前使用哪類 pH 量測方案？如果要切換為 Single-use probe，需要完成哪些驗證工作？
  2. 當 Sensor Spots 的準確度不符合製程要求時，你的風險評估應涵蓋哪些面向？
2.3.2 Single-Use Valves （單次使用閥門）

原文內容 Original Text

Opening and closing of flow paths on SUSs is typically performed using manual or automatic pinch valves. The two main types of automated pinch valves are:

  • Pneumatic pinch valves: Typically used for larger inner diameter (ID) tubing and can hold back greater pressures
  • Solenoid valves: Smaller and do not require the system to be supplied with instrument air (usually 90–100 psi)

Pressure control valves are simply pinch valves controlled by a stepper motor, such that they have thousands of positions rather than just open and closed. Due to the stepper motor function, solenoid pinch valves have greater versatility than pneumatic valves.

Single-use diaphragm-style valves are also available.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：流路控制的設計邏輯

SUT 的閥門設計圍繞一個核心原則：管路就是閥門。透過夾壓柔性管路來實現流路開關，無需任何接觸製程流體的金屬零件。

  • 氣動夾管閥 (Pneumatic pinch valve)：適合大管徑、高壓差，需要廠務提供壓縮空氣（90–100 psi）
  • 電磁夾管閥 (Solenoid valve)：體積小，不需壓縮空氣，但承壓能力較低
  • 步進馬達壓力控制閥：千段位置控制，可做精細流量調節，比氣動閥更靈活

重點提示

SUT 系統通常沒有真正的壓力額定值（與不鏽鋼管路不同），這意味著管路及閥門的壓力承受能力必須在設計階段仔細評估。若壓力超過管路承受極限，可能導致破袋或管路爆裂，是 SUT 實施的重要安全考量。

CDMO 應用情境

在 aseptic fill-finish 前處理（如配製、過濾）流路中，電磁夾管閥因不需壓縮空氣管路配置，可讓整個 SU 配製系統更容易「模組化移動」，搭配輪式支架可靈活配置在不同生產套房內。

2.3.3 Pumps （泵浦）

原文內容 Original Text

2.3.3.1 Pump Types

Positive displacement pumps are typically used in situations where accurate flow control is required while handling fluids sensitive to shear. The main pump types commonly used in single-use applications are peristaltic pumps, diaphragm pumps, and centrifugal pumps.

Peristaltic pumps operate with flexible tubing. The wear of the tubing will cause a slight drift in accuracy; if better flow control over time is needed, a flowmeter can be installed to control pump speed. The peristaltic pump is more flexible and requires less labor.

Diaphragm pumps can provide higher operating pressures and higher flow rates than a typical peristaltic pump. They can also operate for longer continuous periods.

In certain perfusion systems, single-use centrifugal pumps may be used. These will not build up pressure to the point of mechanical failure of the SUS, but will vary flow with pressure changes (e.g., filter loading).

2.3.3.2 Typical Materials of Construction

There is a large variety of tubing materials for peristaltic pumps; selection should be made with the fluid product as a primary consideration. For diaphragm pumps, construction materials are similar to soft goods in traditional stainless steel systems (e.g., housing PP, O-rings EPDM, diaphragms TPE).

2.3.3.3 Selection of Tubing/Diaphragms

Due to operating principles of positive displacement pumps, there are pulsations in pressure and flow that can cause stress on shear sensitive fluids.

For peristaltic pumps, tubing selection is a delicate balance:

  • Larger diameter tubing at a given flow rate operates at lower RPM — yields less frequent pulsations and lower shear; however, lower velocity can cause air to be trapped
  • Selecting pumps with multiple channels also mitigates pulsation

Additional considerations for tubing/diaphragm selection:

  • Dimensional consistency: Pump tubing must maintain its shape under repeated squeezing to ensure consistent flow rate vs. RPM correlation
  • E&L: Leachables testing should be done under operating conditions since tubing is squeezed, stretched, and stressed
  • Spallation: Fragmentation of material during use must be confirmed under process conditions. Recycling fluid to the pump concentrates any spalled material, making it more detectable
  • Compatibility with sterilization conditions: Autoclaving or gamma irradiation can stiffen material and modify the flow rate–pump speed correlation. Characterization after sterilization is strongly recommended

2.3.3.4 Overall Selection Criteria for Pumps

Recommendations for single-use pump package selection include:

  • Material compatibility with fluid
  • Accuracy of flow rate: A balance must be struck for each process
  • Minimum pulsation and stable flow rate: Pulsations challenge stability and strain components
  • Ease of replacement: After every run, quick and error-free reassembly is key
  • Synergy with other SUS components: E.g., different size tubing provides flexibility with pinch valves at higher flow rates

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：泵浦類型選擇邏輯

生物技術流體（特別是含活細胞或蛋白質的流體）對剪切力 (Shear Stress) 高度敏感。正排量泵（Positive Displacement Pump）以容積推動流體，對流體的剪切傷害遠低於離心泵。

  • 蠕動泵 (Peristaltic)：最常用、最靈活，管路是唯一接觸流體的部分，更換簡單
  • 隔膜泵 (Diaphragm)：高流量、長時間連續操作，適合大批量轉移
  • 離心泵 (Centrifugal)：適合灌流系統，不會累積壓力至導致破袋

比喻說明：Spallation（材料碎裂）

就像橡皮筋用久了表面開始掉橡膠屑——蠕動泵管路長時間被滾輪反覆擠壓，材料疲勞後可能產生微小碎片進入製程流體。在生物製藥無菌製造中，這是嚴重的污染風險，必須用製程條件（而非純水）來評估 spallation 特性。

重點提示：Gamma 照射對泵管的影響

Gamma 照射滅菌會讓多種塑料（特別是 PVC、EPDM 等彈性體）硬化 (Stiffening)。硬化後的管路在相同 RPM 下流量與原先不同——出廠前建立的流量–轉速校正曲線可能失效。ISPE 建議在照射後重新評估流量特性，並在工藝確認中納入此考量。

泵浦脈衝控制框架

蠕動泵脈衝控制策略：
  ↑ 管徑 → ↓ RPM → ↓ 脈衝頻率 → ↓ 剪切力
              但 → ↓ 流速 → 空氣滯留風險↑
  多通道泵頭 → 脈衝互相抵消 → 更平滑流量

隔膜泵脈衝控制策略：
  多個小隔膜交替動作 → 脈衝相位分散 → 流量更平穩

CDMO 應用情境：批次切換

SUT 蠕動泵最大優勢：管路更換不需要 CIP/SIP——直接換新管路即完成批次切換。但要注意每批更換管路後，必須重新確認泵速–流量關聯性（新管路的尺寸有批間差異）。在 GMP 環境中，這個確認步驟應記錄於 BPR 中。

2.3.4 Bioreactors （生物反應器）

原文內容 Original Text

2.3.4.1 Design

The primary application of single-use bioreactors is mammalian cell culture. Single-use bioreactors have had limited applicability with microbial cell lines due to limitations in vessel pressure, mass transfer, and venting. Microbial cell lines also present a challenge when the culture becomes heat generating, requiring a jacketed vessel with cooling capabilities.

Bioreactors are equipped with vent filters and filter heaters to promote evaporation of condensate. Even with heaters, filters may be blocked with condensate from exhaust gases, potentially resulting in overpressure, process stops, and potential breach of the bioreactor bag.

For inoculation or harvesting, all transfers should be performed by pumping since overpressure is not possible. This is a critical point for cells sensitive to shear stress.

Ease of use is an important consideration. As the bags are sensitive and complex setup/operations are required, end-users should be sufficiently trained. Factors to consider include: setup and removal time, number of personnel required, and the weight of the new and emptied bag.

Bioreactor designs range from mirroring traditional stainless steel bioreactors to novel agitation mechanisms. Options are still relatively limited with regard to impeller design, impeller size, and sparger type.

2.3.4.2 Process Transfer/Scale-Up

Single-use bioreactors should be characterized prior to use; a robust scaling factor should be selected for the scale-up strategy. Parameters may need to be adjusted since configuration options are more limited compared to stainless steel bioreactors. The recommended practice is to use an equivalent characterized small-scale model.

Considerations for applying conventional scale-up approaches include matching:

  • Geometric ratio (volume/surface) to retain equivalence between scales
  • Oxygen Transfer Rate (OTR) coefficient (kLa) — kept constant if possible
  • Power input per unit volume (P/V, in kW/m³)
  • Volumetric gas flow rate per unit volume (VVM)
  • Mixing time — an important consideration for pH adjustment

Other approaches: constant volumetric scale-up to maintain shear stress; constant tip speed; constant VVM correlated to theoretical kLa.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：為何 SU 生物反應器主要用於哺乳類細胞

哺乳類細胞培養（如 CHO 細胞生產單株抗體）對壓力容忍度低、剪切敏感，需要低速攪拌和溫和的氣液傳質——這正是 SU 生物反應器的設計「甜蜜點」。

微生物發酵（大腸桿菌、酵母菌）則相反：需要高溶氧傳遞效率（OTR）、高攪拌速度、大量排熱，這些都需要堅固的金屬容器，SU 袋體很難滿足。

比喻說明：Vent Filter 冷凝水堵塞

Vent filter 排氣過濾器被冷凝水堵住，就像排水管被油脂堵塞——系統內壓力無處宣洩，最終可能導致袋體破裂。Filter heater 的作用就像給排水管加熱保溫，讓水蒸氣保持氣態而不凝結成液態。這是 SU 生物反應器設計中容易忽略但非常重要的細節。

放大關鍵參數（Scale-Up Parameters）

kLa（體積氧傳遞係數）= 最核心的放大基準
  → 保持 kLa 不變，確保相同的溶氧供給能力

P/V（單位體積功率輸入，kW/m³）
  → 代表攪拌強度，影響混合均勻性與剪切力

VVM（每分鐘氣體體積/液體體積）
  → 控制通氣量，影響 kLa 和 CO₂ 移除

Mixing Time（混合時間）
  → pH 調整時的鹼液混合效率，
     避免局部 pH 過高損傷細胞

重點提示：SU 生物反應器的放大限制

相比傳統不鏽鋼反應器，SU 生物反應器的攪拌器設計、葉輪尺寸和分氣器類型選項非常有限。這意味著放大時可能需要接受工藝參數的妥協（例如無法完全維持相同的 kLa），而不是把傳統系統的參數直接移植過來。

CDMO 應用情境

在 CDMO 接受新客戶工藝時，如果客戶原本使用不鏽鋼生物反應器，轉換到 SU 生物反應器需要進行小規模等效性研究。ISPE 建議的方法是：先用特性化的小規模 SU 模型驗證放大規則，再在商業規模執行。這個研究結果必須記錄並納入工藝驗證計畫。

2.3.5–2.3.6 Chromatography & Ultrafiltration （色層分析與超過濾）

原文內容 Original Text

2.3.5 Chromatography

Chromatography skids with single-use flow paths generally use peristaltic pumps and thus are not suitable for gradient elution, limiting use to binding/elution or flow-through chromatography operations.

This area of SUT is rapidly changing with advancements in continuous processing, in-line dilution, and in-line conditioning. These technologies often lower flow rates to within SUT limits. However, single-use components may not be compatible with concentrated solutions; end-users should consult with suppliers prior to using single-use assemblies with highly concentrated solutions.

2.3.6 Ultrafiltration

Single-use ultrafiltration membranes/systems are available; however, the vast majority of medium to large scale ultrafiltration systems remain multiple-use. This is mainly due to the cost of the membranes, flow limitations through single-use tubing, and the need to spread cost over multiple batches. As a result, single-use ultrafiltration tends to be restricted to smaller scale and niche applications.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：色層分析 SUT 化的限制

色層分析是目前 SUT 化程度最低的下游純化單元操作之一。原因：

  • 梯度洗脫 (Gradient Elution) 需要精準的多路緩衝液混合，蠕動泵的脈衝特性難以勝任
  • 大規模操作（管柱直徑 > 80 cm）所需流量遠超 SU 管路承壓和流量限制
  • 重複使用 vs 拋棄：色層管柱填料非常昂貴，一次性使用的經濟賬算不過來

重點提示：高濃度溶液的相容性

連續製程和 in-line 稀釋技術降低了流量要求，讓更多步驟有機會 SUT 化。但 ISPE 特別提醒：高濃度溶液（高濃度鹽、有機溶劑）可能與 SU 材料不相容，終端使用者在採用前必須先與供應商確認相容性。

超過濾 SUT 化的困境

超過濾膜很昂貴，每次用完就丟——就像每次做義大利麵都換一個新的義大利麵機，完全不符合經濟邏輯。大規模 UF 系統仍以多次使用為主。SU 超過濾只有在小規模或特殊場景（如高活性物質防交叉污染）才具有經濟合理性。

2.3.7 Environmental Requirements （環境需求）

原文內容 Original Text

The ISPE Baseline® Guide: Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities defines three categories of processing:

  • Open process: A process exposed to the environment, requiring environmental conditions to mitigate contamination risk.
  • Closed process: A process system designed and operated such that the product is never exposed to the surrounding environment. Additions to and draws from closed systems need to be performed in a completely closed fashion.
  • Functionally closed process: Process systems that may be opened but are rendered closed by a cleaning, sanitization, and/or sterilization process appropriate to the process requirements (sterile, aseptic, or low bioburden). These systems remain closed during production.

SUSs that use ready-to-use flow paths with aseptic connections are compatible with the reduced environmental requirements of closed or functionally closed operations. A process closure risk assessment should be performed to identify the required classification and segregation needed for different process steps.

Hybrid systems, such as a stainless steel vessel connected to a single-use flow path, are a typical application. A system that has any clean-and-reuse portion should be cleaned, closed, and returned to its sterile state. If the system can be returned to its closed sterile state, it could be reconnected to single-use components and operated in an area with lower area classification as a functionally closed system. The stainless steel vessel could be connected via a steam-through connector, cleaned, and steamed in place (SIP). Once through a SIP cycle, the connection is engaged and the hybrid system is both sterile (or bioburden controlled) and closed.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：製程封閉性決定潔淨室等級需求

這是 SUT 最重要的成本節約機制之一：封閉製程可以在較低等級的潔淨室中操作。

  • 開放製程：產品暴露於環境 → 需要高等級潔淨室（ISO 5 / Grade A）
  • 封閉製程：完全不暴露 → 可降至 ISO 8 甚至 CNC（Controlled Not Classified）
  • 功能性封閉：中間狀態 → 視製程性質，通常 ISO 7 或 ISO 8

關鍵工具：製程封閉性風險評估 (Process Closure Risk Assessment) 必須為每個製程步驟分別評估，不能一刀切。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像水在管道中傳輸（封閉製程）vs. 在開放容器中傳遞（開放製程）。管道裡的水不在乎外面的空氣多髒；但一旦要倒入開放容器，就需要乾淨的操作環境。SUT 的「封閉性」讓你把很多步驟的操作環境從「手術室」降級到「一般醫院走廊」——省下大量設施成本。

重點提示：Hybrid System 的管理原則

不鏽鋼容器 + 單次使用流路的混合系統很常見，但要特別注意：不鏽鋼部分需要按照傳統多次使用設備管理（CIP/SIP），完成 SIP 後才能連接到 SU 流路，整個系統才構成「功能性封閉」。兩個世界的管理規則不能混用，必須在 SOP 中明確區分。

CDMO 應用情境：廠房設計節省

封閉製程讓相當多的上游步驟（培養基配製、緩衝液製備）可在較低等級區域完成，大幅降低潔淨室建設和維護成本。這是新建生物製藥 CDMO 幾乎都以 SUT 為核心的原因——不是因為 SU 耗材便宜，而是因為它讓整個廠房設計成本更低。

2.3.8–2.3.10 Control Systems, Utilities, Maintenance, Safety & Cleaning （控制系統、廠務、維護、安全與清潔）

原文內容 Original Text

2.3.8 Control Systems

Skid manufacturers should follow Good Automated Manufacturing Practice (GAMP®), use modern Open Platform Communications (OPC), and allow open standards to end-users — since closed systems prohibit inclusion into a GMP area.

Additional recommendations:

  • Automation should enable end-users to handle multiple scales
  • The system should display process and system operational parameters with a feedback loop for every control parameter (e.g., agitation should verify motor speed to set point)
  • The control system should include a network interface card and a batch manager
  • Connectivity to the network should be considered since the lighter weight of SUSs allows for more mobility (e.g., a single-use mixer wheeled between locations requires data ports at both locations or a wireless radio)

2.3.9 Utility and Process Support

Electrical: Main electrical load contributions are motors and temperature control. Unlike stainless steel skidded systems, electrical connections on SUSs are typically cord and plug, enabling reconfiguration within a suite.

Process Gases: The lack of a true pressure rating on SUSs may require different gassing/venting control schemes from equivalent stainless steel systems.

Water: For smaller scale operations, bagged water prepared off-site may eliminate purified water lines. For larger scale, water systems typically have fewer use points. Due to temperature sensitivity of SUSs, ambient vs. hot distribution loops with coolers should be evaluated.

Drains: Leveraging the closed system abilities of SUSs could allow systems in a classification that allows an open drain. Decrease in CIP activities may reduce pH neutralization demands.

2.3.10 Maintenance and Calibration

Maintenance requirements are generally reduced for SUSs. Skid manufacturers should: include automated pinch valve cycle counts in automation; allow easy access to single-use components; arrange tubing/connectors/filters for accessibility with sufficient support.

Supplier calibration can be used for single-use components, possibly coupled with on-site post-use calibration. Suppliers should be compliant with ISO/IEC 17025 or equivalent and provide transmitter calibration procedures as part of the turnover package.

2.3.10.1 Safety

Additional safety aspects for SUSs beyond standard E-stops include:

  • Secondary containment to capture leaks during system disassembly
  • Biosafety considerations and containment/inactivation procedures
  • Pressure sensors providing feedback to pump motors to prevent leakage due to bag/plastic rupture
